     4. Procedure for minimum credit requirement

   - Type: Document
   - Format: A4 report (format not specified)

   - Type: Role

7. **系主任**
   - Type: Role
   - Description: Department head who also approves requests.

   - Type: Administrative Unit
   - Description: Office responsible for registration and related processes.

9. **學士班**
   - Type: Educational Program
   - Description: Bachelor program which needs to meet general education credit requirements.

10. **超 (減) 修學分申請表**
    - Type: Application Form
    - Description: Form for applying for extra or reduced credits.

Relationships:
1. **選課確認階段** is open during **開放期間** for **受理對象** (全校學生).
2. Students who do not confirm their course selection cannot raise objections regarding errors.
3. Students who find multiple course selections must opt for online withdrawal instead of application for abandoning courses.
4. Students affected by course changes must write a **報告書** and get it approved by **授課老師** and **系主任** before processing with **註冊組**.
5. Students who do not meet minimum credit requirements and do not select additional courses need to submit **超 (減) 修學分申請表** to **註冊組** after approval. 
6. **選課** is conducted via a **課程資訊及選課系統** which requires confirmation of results.
7. Students with insufficient fusion general education credits must print an application form and submit it to **註冊組** after confirmation.

  - 英文模組 (English Module)

### Relationships
- **Participants to Event**: 全校學士班學生 are the target audience for 第 3 階段選課.
- **Dates to Event**: Multiple dates are related to the course selection process, including registration, announcements, and lotteries.
- **Process to Completion**: Students must log into the system, check their course schedule, and follow procedures for registering for courses based on the distribution results.
- **Requirements**: Students who have not passed required English courses are not allowed to retake the same course.
- **Support**: Students with questions can contact the 外語中心 at extension 52273.
- **Special Circumstances**: Newly transferred, returning, and exchange students have the option of choosing English module levels freely.
- **Registration Process**: Students must apply for changes in modules at the Language Center during weeks 5-17 of the semester if they have higher CEFR test certificates. 
- **Course Withdrawal**: Students wishing to drop courses must do so during the specified online withdrawal period.

   - 9/13 (Computer lottery)
   - 9/16 (Announcement of lottery results)
   - 9/19 (Further unspecified action)

Relationships:
1. Course registration:
   - Students can register for courses but are limited to one A1/A7 or A2 course due to restrictions on the selection process.
   - If a student has already registered for a course of the same type, subsequent registrations for that course type will be invalid.

2. Course conflict:
   - If there is a timetable conflict between registered courses or between registered and previously selected courses, those registrations become invalid.

3. Credit limits:
   - Students exceeding 25 credits or having exceptional academic performance, dual majors, minors, or educational program qualifications, are not allowed to register for more than 31 credits; registrations will still be invalid.

4. Lottery process:
   - Students without A9 General Education courses in their schedule have priority in the lottery process, but having priority does not guarantee higher chances of winning a spot in the course (example provided with numerical probability).

5. Course selection changes:
   - The selection limits may change before the 9/12 deadline, and students must be aware of these changes.

6. Lottery results:
   - Lottery results will be announced on 9/16; students can choose to drop courses during the designated period afterward.

3. **Restrictions on Course Selection for Leave Students**:
   - 1 年級以外的休學生可加、減跨選本系的課程 (Students on leave above the first year can add or reduce courses in their department).
   - 不可跨班選課 (Cannot select courses across different classes/groups).

4. **Course Access by Phases**:
   - 第一階段不受理的科目需等到第二階段開放才可選課 (Subjects that are not available in the first phase can only be selected in the second phase). 

5. **Cross-Year Course Selection Policy**:
   - 休學生可以跨選本系的特定年級課程，但不包括跨班 (Students on leave can select specific grade courses within their department but cannot cross classes/groups).

5. Students must complete the signing approval process after filling out the 超 (減)修 application form.
6. If a course is not in the selected system or the time is unset, students must refer to the 開課單位's announcements and procedures for course selection.
7. Students cannot drop courses after they have commenced in 軟性密集課程, but they can withdraw during the course duration.

   - 25% of lottery slots reserved for students in their third or fourth year.

   - Open to male students to fulfill military service requirements.
   - New students use a lottery system, while continuing students can directly select.

5. **A1 Course:**
   - All students must register for mandatory English module courses in the third lottery stage.

6. **Second Foreign Language Course:**
   - Identified with the same A1 code, applicable to both undergraduate and graduate students.

   - 學士班學生僅能受理本班和本組的課程。
   - 轉系或轉學的學生可跨修本系不同年級的課程，但不能跨班/組。
   - 輔系或雙主修的學生可跨修相關系的課程，但一年級新生課程除外。
   - 休學生可加、減跨選本系1個年級課程，但是不能跨班選課。

3. **分組因素**
   - 建築系因分組，因此二年級和三年級休學復學生的修課選擇有特定限制。

4. **學期升級制**
   - 學士班的學生在升級時除一年級以外，可跨選本系1個年級課程。

5. **全校課程選擇**
   - 不分系學生可跨系選修同年級的課程，但需根據限選條件。

   - 全校不分系學生可跨系加選相同年級之畢業可取得學位系所課程 → (Non-departmental students may select courses across departments for the same grade that lead to graduation)
   - 碩士 (碩專)、博士生僅能選本所課程 → (Master’s and Doctoral students can only select courses from their own department)
   - 跨所選課需於第 2 階段網路選課 → (Cross-department course selection must happen in Phase 2)

2. **選擇階段 (Selection Phases)**
   - 第 1 階段選課開放 → (Course selection for Phase 1 is open)
   - 第 2 階段網上選課 → (Online course selection for Phase 2)
   - 第 3 階段網上選課 → (Online course selection for Phase 3)

3. **修課年級 (Eligible Grades)**
   - 休學復學生可修 1 個年級課程 → (Returning students may take courses from one grade level below or above)
   - 全校不分系 2 年級學生可修 2 年級電機系課程 → (All non-departmental 2nd-year students can take 2nd-year EE courses)

4. **限選條件 (Selection Limitations)**
   - 課程若有限選條件 須遵從規定 → (If a course has selection limitations, students must follow the rules)

   - 一年級新生 (Freshmen)

3. **Course Types:**
   - 必修課程 (Required Courses)
   - 選修課程 (Elective Courses)

4. **抽籤 (Lottery) Mechanisms:**
   - 平均權重亂數抽籤規則 (Weighted Random Lottery Rule)
   - 電腦抽籤 (Computer Lottery)

5. **抽籤名額比例 (Lottery Quota Ratios):**
   - 73% (二年級以上舊生)
   - 27% (一年級新生)
   - 25% (三、四年級以上)

#### Relationships:
- A9 -> No A9 course students are prioritized, 73% of lottery slots reserved for 二年級以上舊生 (Sophomores and above).
- A7 -> Mandatory for students who have not completed 4 credits, maximum of 1 course can be drawn.
- A2 -> Students with incomplete 4 credit courses can register interest; priority given to freshmen; 25% of slots for 三、四年級 (third or fourth year students).
- A3 -> Open to male students for military service; new students use computer lottery, continuing students select directly.
- A1 -> All students must register for mandatory English module courses in the third lottery stage.
- Second Foreign Language Course (A1) -> Applicable to both undergraduate and graduate students. 

### Summary:
This structured summary outlines the rules and priorities for course selection and lottery mechanisms for various student classes at a university, detailing specific courses, requirements, and the allocation of lottery slots amongst students from different years.

4. 學士一年級錄取新生及暑假轉學正取新生 -> 第 2 階段選課 (First-year undergraduate new students and transfers in summer have different rules in Phase 2 Course Selection)
5. 此階段 -> 本系 (所) and 本年級 / 組班選課 (This phase ensures course selections are related to the department and the respective grade/class)
6. 必修課程 -> 本系本年級 (Required courses are subject to internal designation for students of the same department and year, while elective courses have department-based limits)
7. 第１階段網路選課 -> 開放期間 (A specific time period is established for Phase 1 Online Course Selection: July 15, 09:00 ~ July 19, 17:00)
Element index 27 of 31:
Element summary: **Entities:**

1. **課程 (Courses)**
   - 必修課程 (Required Courses)
   - 選修課程 (Elective Courses)
   - 分班課程 (Class-based Courses)
   - 分組課程 (Group-based Courses)

2. **學生類別 (Student Categories)**
   - 學士班學生 (Bachelor's Degree Students)
   - 轉系學生 (Transfer Students)
   - 轉學學生 (Transferring Students)
   - 輔系學生 (Minor Students)
   - 雙主修學生 (Double Major Students)
   - 休學生 (Students on Leave)

3. **年級 (Grade Levels)**
   - 一年級 (1st Year)
   - 二年級 (2nd Year)
   - 三年級 (3rd Year)
   - 四年級 (4th Year)

4. **系所 (Departments)**
   - 數學系 (Department of Mathematics)
   - 機械系 (Department of Mechanical Engineering)
   - 建築系 (Department of Architecture)

**Relationships:**

1. 課程 (Courses) -> 必修課程 (Required Courses): 無限選名額限制。
2. 課程 (Courses) -> 選修課程 (Elective Courses): 依系所設定限選名額；若設定為不限者，則無名額限制。
3. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 學士班學生 (Bachelor's Degree Students): 僅能受理本班和本組的課程。
4. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 轉系學生 (Transfer Students): 可跨修本系不同年級的課程，但不能跨班/組。
5. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 輔系學生 (Minor Students): 可跨修相關系的課程，但一年級新生課程除外。
6. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 雙主修學生 (Double Major Students): 可跨修相關系的課程，但一年級新生課程除外。
7. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 休學生 (Students on Leave): 可加、減跨選本系1個年級課程，但不能跨班選課。
8. 系所 (Departments) -> 建築系 (Department of Architecture): 二年級和三年級休學復學生的修課選擇有特定限制。
9. 學級 (Grade Levels) -> 學士班學生 (Bachelor's Degree Students): 除一年級以外，在升級時可跨選本系1個年級課程。
10. 學生類別 (Student Categories) -> 全校課程選擇: 不分系學生可跨系選修同年級的課程，但需根據限選條件。
Element index 28 of 31:
Element summary: ### Entities:
1. **年級 (Grade)**
   - 3 年級 (Grade 3)
   - 2 年級 (Grade 2)
   - 1 年級 (Grade 1)
   - 4 年級 (Grade 4)

2. **班級 (Class)**
   - 甲班 (Class A)
   - 乙班 (Class B)

3. **學生狀態 (Student Status)**
   - 休學 (Leave of Absence)
   - 復學生 (Returning Student)

4. **系所 (Department)**
   - 電機系 (Department of Electrical Engineering)
   - 電資學院 (College of Electrical and Computer Engineering)
   - 碩士 (Master)
   - 碩專 (Professional Master's)
   - 博士生 (Doctoral Student)

5. **課程類型 (Course Type)**
   - 必修課程 (Required Courses)
   - 選修課程 (Elective Courses)

6. **階段 (Phase)**
   - 第 1 階段 (Phase 1)
   - 第 2 階段 (Phase 2)
   - 第 3 階段 (Phase 3)

7. **課程查詢 (Course Inquiry)**
   - 系代號 (Department Code)
   - A1, A3, A4, A5, A6, AA, AH (Various Department Codes)

### Relationships:
1. **選課規則 (Course Selection Rules)**
   - 3 年級休學復學生可修 2 年級甲乙班課程 -> Grade 3 students on leave can take Grade 2 Class A or B courses
   - 全校不分系學生可跨系加選相同年級之畢業可取得學位系所課程 -> Non-departmental students may select courses across departments for the same grade that lead to graduation
   - 碩士 (碩專)、博士生僅能選本所課程 -> Master’s and Doctoral students can only select courses from their own department
   - 跨所選課需於第 2 階段網路選課 -> Cross-department course selection must happen in Phase 2

2. **選擇階段 (Selection Phases)**
   - 第 1 階段選課開放 -> Course selection for Phase 1 is open
   - 第 2 階段網上選課 -> Online course selection for Phase 2
   - 第 3 階段網上選課 -> Online course selection for Phase 3

3. **修課年級 (Eligible Grades)**
   - 休學復學生可修 1 個年級課程 -> Returning students may take courses from one grade level below or above
   - 全校不分系 2 年級學生可修 2 年級電機系課程 -> All non-departmental 2nd-year students can take 2nd-year EE courses

4. **限選條件 (Selection Limitations)**
   - 課程若有限選條件 須遵從規定 -> If a course has selection limitations, students must follow the rules

**Relationships:**

- 學士班舊生 (Undergraduate Students) -> 包括 -> 復學生 (Returning Students)

- 學士班舊生 (Undergraduate Students) -> 可於 -> 開放期間 (Open Registration Period) 進行網路選課
- 每項志願選項課程 (Course Preference Options) -> 至多可抽中 -> 1 科 (One Course)
- 若遇到抽中志願課程衝堂 (Scheduling Conflicts), 學生需於網路棄選開放時段自行棄選 (Self-Drop During Drop Period)
- 通識課程 (General Education) A9 及 大學國文 (University Chinese) A7 -> 必須依照 -> 志願序 (Preference Order) 及 抽籤規則 (Lottery Rules) 進行選擇
